    18‚Üí  asChild?: boolean;
    19‚Üí  /** Icon to display on the left side */
    20‚Üí  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
    21‚Üí  /** Icon to display on the right side */
    22‚Üí  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
    23‚Üí  /** Show loading state */
    24‚Üí  loading?: boolean;
    25‚Üí}
    26‚Üí
    27‚Üí/**
    28‚Üí * A premium glass-effect button component with advanced visual effects.
    29‚Üí *
    30‚Üí * Features:
    31‚Üí * - Multiple variants (primary, secondary, tertiary, ghost, destructive)
    32‚Üí * - 5 size options (xs, sm, md, lg, xl)
    33‚Üí * - Loading states with spinner
    34‚Üí * - Left and right icons
    35‚Üí * - Glass morphism effects with backdrop blur
    36‚Üí * - Magnetic hover interactions
    37‚Üí * - Haptic feedback support
    38‚Üí * - Accessibility compliant
    39‚Üí *
    40‚Üí * @example
    41‚Üí * \```tsx
    42‚Üí * <GlassButton variant="primary" size="md" leftIcon={<PlayIcon />}>
    43‚Üí *   Play Video
    44‚Üí * </GlassButton>
    45‚Üí * \```
    46‚Üí */
    47‚Üíconst GlassButton = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, GlassButtonProps>(
    48‚Üí  (
    49‚Üí    {
    50‚Üí      className,
    51‚Üí      variant = 'primary',
    52‚Üí      size = 'md',
    53‚Üí      asChild = false,
    54‚Üí      leftIcon,
    55‚Üí      rightIcon,
    56‚Üí      loading = false,
    57‚Üí      disabled,
    58‚Üí      children,
    59‚Üí      ...props
    60‚Üí    },
    61‚Üí    ref
    62‚Üí  ) => {
    63‚Üí    const [isPressed, setIsPressed] = useState(false);
    64‚Üí    const internalButtonRef = useRef<HTMLButtonElement | null>(null);
    65‚Üí    const { magneticHover, specularHighlights } = useLiquidGlass();
    66‚Üí    const { elementRef: magneticRef, transform } = useMagneticHover(0.3, 120);
    67‚Üí    const { measureGlassInteraction } = useGlassEffectPerformance('Button');
    68‚Üí
    69‚Üí    // Callback ref to handle both internal and external refs, including magnetic ref
    70‚Üí    const setRefs = useCallback(
    71‚Üí      (node: HTMLButtonElement | null) => {
    72‚Üí        // Set internal ref
    73‚Üí        if (internalButtonRef.current !== node) {
    74‚Üí          (
    75‚Üí            internalButtonRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>
    76‚Üí          ).current = node;
    77‚Üí        }
    78‚Üí        // Assign to magnetic ref if enabled
    79‚Üí        if (magneticHover && magneticRef && 'current' in magneticRef) {
    80‚Üí          (magneticRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>).current =
    81‚Üí            node;
    82‚Üí        }
    83‚Üí        // Assign to forwarded ref
    84‚Üí        if (typeof ref === 'function') {
    85‚Üí          ref(node);
    86‚Üí        } else if (ref && 'current' in ref) {
    87‚Üí          (ref as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>).current =
    88‚Üí            node;
    89‚Üí        }
    90‚Üí      },
    91‚Üí      [magneticHover, magneticRef, ref]
    92‚Üí    );
    93‚Üí
    94‚Üí    const handleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLButtonElement>) => {
    95‚Üí      const endMeasure = measureGlassInteraction('click');
    96‚Üí
    97‚Üí      if (internalButtonRef.current && !disabled && !loading) {
    98‚Üí        const rect = internalButtonRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    99‚Üí        const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
   100‚Üí        const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
   101‚Üí        createGlassRipple(
   102‚Üí          internalButtonRef.current,
   103‚Üí          x,
   104‚Üí          y,
   105‚Üí          'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)'
   106‚Üí        );
   107‚Üí      }
   108‚Üí
   109‚Üí      props.onClick?.(e);
   110‚Üí      endMeasure();
   111‚Üí    };
   112‚Üí
   113‚Üí    const baseClasses = cn(
   114‚Üí      'liquid-glass liquid-interactive font-medium rounded-xl relative overflow-hidden',
   115‚Üí      'focus:outline-none liquid-glass-focus liquid-glass-ripple', // Ensure liquid-glass-focus provides a visible focus ring
   116‚Üí      microInteraction.smooth,
   117‚Üí      'disabled:opacity-60 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:transform-none',
   118‚Üí      specularHighlights && 'liquid-glass-specular liquid-glass-shimmer',
   119‚Üí      magneticHover && 'liquid-magnetic',
   120‚Üí      isPressed && 'scale-[0.98] brightness-95'
   121‚Üí    );
   122‚Üí
   123‚Üí    const variantClasses = {
   124‚Üí      primary: cn(
   125‚Üí        'text-white dark:text-white font-semibold',
   126‚Üí        'bg-gradient-to-b',
   127‚Üí        'from-blue-500 to-blue-600', // Fallback colors
   128‚Üí        'hover:from-blue-400 hover:to-blue-500',
   129‚Üí        'active:from-blue-600 active:to-blue-600',
   130‚Üí        'shadow-lg shadow-blue-500/25',
   131‚Üí        'border border-blue-400/30',
   132‚Üí        // Light theme: dark text on glass background
   133‚Üí        'light:text-slate-800 light:from-white/80 light:to-gray-50/90',
   134‚Üí        'light:hover:from-white/90 light:hover:to-gray-100/95',
   135‚Üí        'light:border-gray-300/50 light:shadow-gray-500/20'
   136‚Üí      ),
   137‚Üí      secondary: cn(
   138‚Üí        'text-gray-900 dark:text-white', // Fallback text colors
   139‚Üí        'border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700', // Fallback border
   140‚Üí        'hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-800',
   141‚Üí        'active:bg-gray-100 dark:active:bg-gray-700'
   142‚Üí      ),
   143‚Üí      tertiary: cn(
   144‚Üí        'text-gray-900 dark:text-white bg-transparent',
   145‚Üí        'hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 hover:backdrop-blur-sm',
   146‚Üí        'active:bg-gray-100 dark:active:bg-gray-700'
   147‚Üí      ),
   148‚Üí      ghost: cn(
   149‚Üí        'text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400 bg-transparent',
   150‚Üí        'hover:text-gray-900 dark:hover:text-white hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-800',
   151‚Üí        'active:bg-gray-100 dark:active:bg-gray-700'
   152‚Üí      ),
   153‚Üí      destructive: cn(
   154‚Üí        'text-white font-semibold',
   155‚Üí        'bg-gradient-to-b from-red-500 to-red-600',
   156‚Üí        'hover:from-red-400 hover:to-red-500',
   157‚Üí        'active:from-red-600 active:to-red-600',
   158‚Üí        'shadow-lg shadow-red-500/25',
   159‚Üí        'border border-red-400/30'
   160‚Üí      ),
   161‚Üí    };
   162‚Üí
   163‚Üí    const sizeClasses = {
   164‚Üí      xs: 'px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs min-h-[28px]',
   165‚Üí      sm: 'px-3 py-2 text-sm min-h-[32px]',
   166‚Üí      md: 'px-4 py-2.5 text-sm min-h-[40px]',
   167‚Üí      lg: 'px-6 py-3 text-base min-h-[44px]',
   168‚Üí      xl: 'px-8 py-4 text-lg min-h-[52px]',
   169‚Üí    };
   170‚Üí
   171‚Üí    const iconSizeClasses = {
   172‚Üí      xs: 'w-3 h-3',
   173‚Üí      sm: 'w-3.5 h-3.5',
   174‚Üí      md: 'w-4 h-4',
   175‚Üí      lg: 'w-5 h-5',
   176‚Üí      xl: 'w-6 h-6',
   177‚Üí    };
   178‚Üí
   179‚Üí    if (asChild) {
   180‚Üí      return (
   181‚Üí        <Slot
   182‚Üí          ref={setRefs}
   183‚Üí          className={cn(
   184‚Üí            baseClasses,
   185‚Üí            variantClasses[variant],
   186‚Üí            sizeClasses[size],
   187‚Üí            className
   188‚Üí          )}
   189‚Üí          style={{
   190‚Üí            transform: magneticHover ? transform : undefined,
   191‚Üí            ...props.style,
   192‚Üí          }}
   193‚Üí          data-disabled={disabled || loading}
   194‚Üí          aria-busy={loading ? true : undefined}
   195‚Üí          onMouseDown={() => setIsPressed(true)}
   196‚Üí          onMouseUp={() => setIsPressed(false)}
   197‚Üí          onMouseLeave={() => setIsPressed(false)}
   198‚Üí          onClick={handleClick}
   199‚Üí          {...props}
   200‚Üí        >
   201‚Üí          {children}
   202‚Üí        </Slot>
   203‚Üí      );
   204‚Üí    }
   205‚Üí
   206‚Üí    return (
   207‚Üí      <button
   208‚Üí        className={cn(
   209‚Üí          baseClasses,
   210‚Üí          variantClasses[variant],
   211‚Üí          sizeClasses[size],
   212‚Üí          className
   213‚Üí        )}
   214‚Üí        ref={setRefs}
   215‚Üí        style={{
   216‚Üí          transform: magneticHover ? transform : undefined,
   217‚Üí          ...props.style,
   218‚Üí        }}
   219‚Üí        disabled={disabled || loading}
   220‚Üí        aria-busy={loading ? true : undefined}
   221‚Üí        onMouseDown={() => setIsPressed(true)}
   222‚Üí        onMouseUp={() => setIsPressed(false)}
   223‚Üí        onMouseLeave={() => setIsPressed(false)}
   224‚Üí        onClick={handleClick}
   225‚Üí        {...props}
   226‚Üí      >
   227‚Üí        {/* Loading state overlay */}
   228‚Üí        {loading && (
   229‚Üí          <div
   230‚Üí            className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-current/10 rounded-xl"
   231‚Üí            aria-hidden="true"
   232‚Üí          >
   233‚Üí            <div
   234‚Üí              className={cn(
   235‚Üí                'animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-current border-t-transparent',
   236‚Üí                iconSizeClasses[size]
   237‚Üí              )}
   238‚Üí            />
   239‚Üí          </div>
   240‚Üí        )}
   241‚Üí
   242‚Üí        <div
   243‚Üí          className={cn(
   244‚Üí            'flex items-center justify-center gap-2',
   245‚Üí            loading && 'opacity-0'
   246‚Üí          )}
   247‚Üí        >
   248‚Üí          {leftIcon && (
   249‚Üí            <span
   250‚Üí              className={cn('flex-shrink-0', iconSizeClasses[size])}
   251‚Üí              aria-hidden="true"
   252‚Üí            >
   253‚Üí              {leftIcon}
   254‚Üí            </span>
   255‚Üí          )}
   256‚Üí          <span className="truncate">{children}</span>
   257‚Üí          {rightIcon && (
   258‚Üí            <span
   259‚Üí              className={cn('flex-shrink-0', iconSizeClasses[size])}
   260‚Üí              aria-hidden="true"
   261‚Üí            >
   262‚Üí              {rightIcon}
   263‚Üí            </span>
   264‚Üí          )}
   265‚Üí        </div>
   266‚Üí      </button>
   267‚Üí    );
   268‚Üí  }
   269‚Üí);
   270‚Üí
   271‚ÜíGlassButton.displayName = 'GlassButton';
   272‚Üí
   273‚Üíexport { GlassButton };
   274‚Üí
```

    98‚Üí        <div className="px-4 py-2 bg-white/25 border-b border-white/15">
    99‚Üí          <h4 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 dark:text-white">
   100‚Üí            {title}
   101‚Üí          </h4>
   102‚Üí        </div>
   103‚Üí      )}
   104‚Üí      <div className="relative">
   105‚Üí        <pre className="p-4 overflow-x-auto text-sm bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-900">
   106‚Üí          <code
   107‚Üí            className={`language-${language} text-gray-900 dark:text-white`}
   108‚Üí          >
   109‚Üí            {code}
   110‚Üí          </code>
   111‚Üí        </pre>
   112‚Üí        <button
   113‚Üí          onClick={copyToClipboard}
   114‚Üí          className="absolute top-2 right-2 p-2 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 hover:text-gray-900 dark:hover:text-white transition-colors rounded-md hover:bg-white/18"
   115‚Üí          title="Copy code"
   116‚Üí        >
   117‚Üí          <svg
   118‚Üí            width="16"
   119‚Üí            height="16"
   120‚Üí            viewBox="0 0 24 24"
   121‚Üí            fill="none"
   122‚Üí            stroke="currentColor"
   123‚Üí            strokeWidth="2"
   124‚Üí          >
   125‚Üí            <rect x="9" y="9" width="13" height="13" rx="2" ry="2"></rect>
   126‚Üí            <path d="M5 15H4a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h9a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v1"></path>
   127‚Üí          </svg>
   128‚Üí        </button>
   129‚Üí      </div>
   130‚Üí    </div>
   131‚Üí  );
   132‚Üí};
   133‚Üí
   134‚Üí// Usage Examples Component
   135‚Üíexport const UsageExample = ({
   136‚Üí  title,
   137‚Üí  description,
   138‚Üí  example,
   139‚Üí  code,
   140‚Üí}: {
   141‚Üí  title: string;
   142‚Üí  description?: string;
   143‚Üí  example: React.ReactNode;
   144‚Üí  code: string;
   145‚Üí}) => {
   146‚Üí  return (
   147‚Üí    <div className="my-8">
   148‚Üí      <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2 text-gray-900 dark:text-white">
   149‚Üí        {title}
   150‚Üí      </h3>
   151‚Üí      {description && (
   152‚Üí        <p className="text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 mb-4">{description}</p>
   153‚Üí      )}
   154‚Üí
   155‚Üí      {/* Live Example */}
   156‚Üí      <div className="liquid-glass rounded-xl p-6 mb-4 border border-white/15">
   157‚Üí        <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-[120px]">
   158‚Üí          {example}
   159‚Üí        </div>
   160‚Üí      </div>
   161‚Üí
   162‚Üí      {/* Code */}
   163‚Üí      <CodeBlock code={code} title="Code" />
   164‚Üí    </div>
   165‚Üí  );
   166‚Üí};
   167‚Üí
   168‚Üí// Feature Badge Component
   169‚Üíexport const FeatureBadge = ({
   170‚Üí  type,
   171‚Üí  children,
   172‚Üí}: {
   173‚Üí  type: 'new' | 'updated' | 'experimental' | 'deprecated';
   174‚Üí  children: React.ReactNode;
   175‚Üí}) => {
   176‚Üí  const styles = {
   177‚Üí    new: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900 dark:text-green-200',
   178‚Üí    updated: 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900 dark:text-blue-200',
   179‚Üí    experimental:
   180‚Üí      'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 dark:bg-yellow-900 dark:text-yellow-200',
   181‚Üí    deprecated: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900 dark:text-red-200',
   182‚Üí  };
   183‚Üí
   184‚Üí  return (
   185‚Üí    <span
   186‚Üí      className={cn(
   187‚Üí        'inline-flex items-center px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium',
   188‚Üí        styles[type]
   189‚Üí      )}
   190‚Üí    >
   191‚Üí      {children}
   192‚Üí    </span>
   193‚Üí  );
   194‚Üí};
   195‚Üí

   236‚Üí// Accessibility Guidelines Component
   237‚Üíexport const AccessibilityGuidelines = ({
   238‚Üí  guidelines,
   239‚Üí}: {
   240‚Üí  guidelines: Array<{
   241‚Üí    title: string;
   242‚Üí    description: string;
   243‚Üí    level: 'A' | 'AA' | 'AAA';
   244‚Üí  }>;
   245‚Üí}) => {
   246‚Üí  const levelColors = {
   247‚Üí    A: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900 dark:text-green-200',
   248‚Üí    AA: 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900 dark:text-blue-200',
   249‚Üí    AAA: 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-800 dark:bg-purple-900 dark:text-purple-200',
   250‚Üí  };
   251‚Üí
   252‚Üí  return (
   253‚Üí    <div className="liquid-glass rounded-xl p-6 my-6 border border-white/15">

   255‚Üí        Accessibility Guidelines
   256‚Üí      </h3>
   257‚Üí      <div className="space-y-4">
   258‚Üí        {guidelines.map((guideline, index) => (
   259‚Üí          <div key={index} className="border-l-2 border-blue-500 pl-4">
   260‚Üí            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
   261‚Üí              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900 dark:text-white">
   262‚Üí                {guideline.title}
   263‚Üí              </h4>
   264‚Üí              <span
   265‚Üí                className={cn(
   266‚Üí                  'px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium',
   267‚Üí                  levelColors[guideline.level]
   268‚Üí                )}
   269‚Üí              >
   270‚Üí                WCAG {guideline.level}
   271‚Üí              </span>
   272‚Üí            </div>
   273‚Üí            <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300">
   274‚Üí              {guideline.description}
   275‚Üí            </p>
   276‚Üí          </div>
   277‚Üí        ))}
   278‚Üí      </div>
   279‚Üí    </div>
   280‚Üí  );
   281‚Üí};

   283‚Üí// Component Status Component
   284‚Üíexport const ComponentStatus = ({
   285‚Üí  status,
   286‚Üí}: {
   287‚Üí  status: 'stable' | 'beta' | 'alpha' | 'deprecated';
   288‚Üí}) => {
   289‚Üí  const statusConfig = {
   290‚Üí    stable: {
   291‚Üí      color:
   292‚Üí        'bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900 dark:text-green-200',
   293‚Üí      icon: '‚úÖ',
   294‚Üí      description: 'Ready for production use',
   295‚Üí    },
   296‚Üí    beta: {
   297‚Üí      color: 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900 dark:text-blue-200',
   298‚Üí      icon: 'üß™',
   299‚Üí      description: 'Feature complete, may have minor changes',
   300‚Üí    },
   301‚Üí    alpha: {
   302‚Üí      color:
   303‚Üí        'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 dark:bg-yellow-900 dark:text-yellow-200',
   304‚Üí      icon: '‚ö†Ô∏è',
   305‚Üí      description: 'Under development, breaking changes possible',
   306‚Üí    },
   307‚Üí    deprecated: {
   308‚Üí      color: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900 dark:text-red-200',
   309‚Üí      icon: 'üö´',
   310‚Üí      description: 'Will be removed in future versions',
   311‚Üí    },
   312‚Üí  };
   313‚Üí
   314‚Üí  const config = statusConfig[status];
   315‚Üí
   316‚Üí  return (
   317‚Üí    <div
   318‚Üí      className={cn(
   319‚Üí        'inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-full text-sm font-medium mb-4',
   320‚Üí        config.color
   321‚Üí      )}
   322‚Üí    >
   323‚Üí      <span>{config.icon}</span>
   324‚Üí      <span>Status: {status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + status.slice(1)}</span>
   325‚Üí      <span className="text-xs opacity-75">‚Äî {config.description}</span>
   326‚Üí    </div>
   327‚Üí  );
   328‚Üí};
   329‚Üí
```

Result:

```

     4‚Üí */

1‚Üí/**
     2‚Üí * Apple Liquid Glass Showcase Page
     3‚Üí * Demonstrates all the new liquid glass effects and patterns
     4‚Üí * Based on authentic Apple design language from GitHub gists
     5‚Üí */

     7‚Üíimport { useState } from 'react';
     8‚Üíimport {

    11‚Üí  AppleLiquidGlassButton,

    15‚Üí
    16‚Üíexport default function AppleLiquidGlassShowcase() {
    17‚Üí  const [selectedIntensity, setSelectedIntensity] = useState<'subtle' | 'medium' | 'strong'>('medium');
    18‚Üí  const [enabledEffects, setEnabledEffects] = useState({
    19‚Üí    magnetic: true,
    20‚Üí    animated: false,
    21‚Üí    multiLayer: true,
    22‚Üí  });
    23‚Üí

    59‚Üí            Effect Controls
    60‚Üí          </h2>
    61‚Üí          
    62‚Üí          <div className="space-y-4">
    63‚Üí            {/* Intensity Control */}

    66‚Üí                Intensity
    67‚Üí              </label>

    69‚Üí                {(['subtle', 'medium', 'strong'] as const).map((intensity) => (

    72‚Üí                    size="sm"
    73‚Üí                    intensity={selectedIntensity === intensity ? 'strong' : 'subtle'}
    74‚Üí                    onClick={() => setSelectedIntensity(intensity)}
    75‚Üí                    className={selectedIntensity === intensity ? 'ring-2 ring-white/50' : ''}
    76‚Üí                  >

    94‚Üí                    onClick={() => setEnabledEffects(prev => ({
    95‚Üí                      ...prev,
    96‚Üí                      [effect]: !prev[effect as keyof typeof prev]
    97‚Üí                    }))}
    98‚Üí                    className={enabled ? 'ring-2 ring-white/50' : ''}
    99‚Üí                  >
   100‚Üí                    {effect.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + effect.slice(1)}

   107‚Üí
   108‚Üí        {/* Glass Components Grid */}

    13‚Üí## Props
    14‚Üí
    15‚Üí| Name | Type | Default | Description |
    16‚Üí|------|------|---------|-------------|
    17‚Üí| title | `string` | ‚Äî | Main hero title text |
    18‚Üí| subtitle | `string` | ‚Äî | Optional subtitle displayed above the title |
    19‚Üí| description | `string` | ‚Äî | Optional description text below the title |
    20‚Üí| primaryAction | `{ label: string; onClick: () => void; icon?: React.ReactNode }` | ‚Äî | Primary call-to-action button configuration |
    21‚Üí| secondaryAction | `{ label: string; onClick: () => void; icon?: React.ReactNode }` | ‚Äî | Secondary action button configuration |
    22‚Üí| backgroundImage | `string` | ‚Äî | Optional background image URL |
    23‚Üí| backgroundVideo | `string` | ‚Äî | Optional background video URL |
    24‚Üí| variant | `'default' \| 'centered' \| 'split' \| 'minimal'` | `'default'` | Layout variant for the hero section |
    25‚Üí| size | `'sm' \| 'md' \| 'lg' \| 'xl'` | `'lg'` | Overall size and spacing of the hero |
    26‚Üí| enableParallax | `boolean` | `true` | Enable parallax background effects |
    27‚Üí| enableMagnetic | `boolean` | `false` | Enable magnetic hover interactions |
    28‚Üí

1‚Üíimport React, { forwardRef, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
     2‚Üíimport { motion, Variants } from 'framer-motion';
     3‚Üíimport { cn } from '@/lib/glass-utils';
     4‚Üíimport { useLiquidGlass, useContentAwareGlass } from '@/hooks/use-liquid-glass';
     5‚Üíimport { useMagneticHover } from '@/lib/glass-physics';
     6‚Üíimport { GlassButton } from './glass-button';
     7‚Üíimport {
     8‚Üí  fadeInUpLarge,
     9‚Üí  containerFadeInFast,
    10‚Üí} from '@/lib/framer-motion-constants';
    11‚Üí
    12‚Üíexport interface GlassHeroProps extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
    13‚Üí  title: string;
    14‚Üí  subtitle?: string;
    15‚Üí  description?: string;
    16‚Üí  primaryAction?: {
    17‚Üí    label: string;
    18‚Üí    onClick: () => void;
    19‚Üí    icon?: React.ReactNode;
    20‚Üí  };
    21‚Üí  secondaryAction?: {
    22‚Üí    label: string;
    23‚Üí    onClick: () => void;
    24‚Üí    icon?: React.ReactNode;
    25‚Üí  };
    26‚Üí  backgroundImage?: string;
    27‚Üí  backgroundVideo?: string;
    28‚Üí  variant?: 'default' | 'centered' | 'split' | 'minimal';
    29‚Üí  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl';
    30‚Üí  enableParallax?: boolean;
    31‚Üí  enableMagnetic?: boolean;
    32‚Üí}
    33‚Üí
    34‚Üíconst GlassHero = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, GlassHeroProps>(
    35‚Üí  (
    36‚Üí    {
    37‚Üí      className,
    38‚Üí      title,
    39‚Üí      subtitle,
    40‚Üí      description,
    41‚Üí      primaryAction,
    42‚Üí      secondaryAction,
    43‚Üí      backgroundImage,
    44‚Üí      backgroundVideo,
    45‚Üí      variant = 'default',
    46‚Üí      size = 'lg',
    47‚Üí      enableParallax = true,
    48‚Üí      enableMagnetic = false,
    49‚Üí      children,
    50‚Üí      ...props
    51‚Üí    },
    52‚Üí    ref
    53‚Üí  ) => {
    54‚Üí    const contentRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
    55‚Üí    const { specularHighlights } = useLiquidGlass();
    56‚Üí    useContentAwareGlass(contentRef as React.RefObject<HTMLElement>);
    57‚Üí    const { elementRef: magneticRef, transform } = useMagneticHover(0.2, 200);
    58‚Üí
    59‚Üí    // Callback ref to handle both content and magnetic refs
    60‚Üíconst setRefs = useCallback((node: HTMLDivElement | null) => {
    61‚Üí      (contentRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>).current = node;
    62‚Üí      if (enableMagnetic && magneticRef) {
    63‚Üí        (magneticRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>).current = node;
    64‚Üí      }
    65‚Üí      if (typeof ref === 'function') {
    66‚Üí        ref(node);
    67‚Üí      } else if (ref) {
    68‚Üí        (ref as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>).current = node;
    69‚Üí      }
    70‚Üí    }, [enableMagnetic, magneticRef, ref]);
    71‚Üí
    72‚Üí    const sizeClasses = {
    73‚Üí      sm: 'min-h-[60vh] py-16 px-6',
    74‚Üí      md: 'min-h-[70vh] py-20 px-8',
    75‚Üí      lg: 'min-h-[80vh] py-24 px-8',
    76‚Üí      xl: 'min-h-[90vh] py-32 px-12',
    77‚Üí    };
    78‚Üí
    79‚Üí    const variantClasses = {
    80‚Üí      default: 'text-center',
    81‚Üí      centered: 'text-center items-center justify-center',
    82‚Üí      split: 'text-left lg:text-left items-center',
    83‚Üí      minimal: 'text-center items-center justify-center py-16',
    84‚Üí    };
    85‚Üí
    86‚Üí    const titleSizes = {
    87‚Üí      sm: 'text-4xl md:text-5xl',
    88‚Üí      md: 'text-5xl md:text-6xl',
    89‚Üí      lg: 'text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl',
    90‚Üí      xl: 'text-7xl md:text-8xl lg:text-9xl',
    91‚Üí    };
    92‚Üí
    93‚Üí    const containerVariants: Variants = containerFadeInFast;
    94‚Üí
    95‚Üí    const itemVariants: Variants = fadeInUpLarge;
    96‚Üí
    97‚Üí    const parallaxVariants = enableParallax
    98‚Üí      ? {
    99‚Üí          initial: { y: 0 },
   100‚Üí          animate: { y: -20 },
   101‚Üí          transition: {
   102‚Üí            duration: 2,
   103‚Üí            repeat: Infinity,
   104‚Üí            repeatType: 'reverse' as const,
   105‚Üí            ease: 'easeInOut' as const,
   106‚Üí          },
   107‚Üí        }
   108‚Üí      : {};
   109‚Üí
   110‚Üí    return (
   111‚Üí      <div
   112‚Üí        ref={setRefs}
   113‚Üí        className={cn(
   114‚Üí          'relative overflow-hidden',
   115‚Üí          'liquid-glass-adaptive liquid-glass-depth-2',
   116‚Üí          specularHighlights && 'liquid-glass-specular',
   117‚Üí          sizeClasses[size],
   118‚Üí          className
   119‚Üí        )}
   120‚Üí        style={{
   121‚Üí          transform: enableMagnetic ? transform : undefined,
   122‚Üí          backgroundImage: backgroundImage
   123‚Üí            ? `url(${backgroundImage})`
   124‚Üí            : 'linear-gradient(135deg, #1a1a1a 0%, #2d2d2d 20%, #4a4a4a 40%, #6b7280 60%, #9ca3af 80%, #e5e7eb 100%)',
   125‚Üí          backgroundSize: backgroundImage ? 'cover' : '400% 400%',
   126‚Üí          backgroundPosition: 'center',
   127‚Üí          backgroundAttachment: enableParallax ? 'fixed' : 'scroll',
   128‚Üí          animation: !backgroundImage
   129‚Üí            ? 'gradientShift 15s ease infinite'
   130‚Üí            : undefined,
   131‚Üí        }}
   132‚Üí        {...props}
   133‚Üí      >
   134‚Üí        {/* Background Video */}
   135‚Üí        {backgroundVideo && (
   136‚Üí          <video
   137‚Üí            autoPlay
   138‚Üí            muted
   139‚Üí            loop
   140‚Üí            playsInline
   141‚Üí            className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full object-cover -z-10"
   142‚Üí          >
   143‚Üí            <source src={backgroundVideo} type="video/mp4" />
   144‚Üí          </video>
   145‚Üí        )}
   146‚Üí
   147‚Üí        {/* Background Overlay */}
   148‚Üí        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-white/5 via-transparent to-black/5 dark:from-black/20 dark:via-transparent dark:to-black/40 -z-5" />
   149‚Üí
   150‚Üí        {/* Animated Background Elements */}
   151‚Üí        <div className="absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden -z-10">
   152‚Üí          <motion.div
   153‚Üí            className="absolute top-1/4 left-1/4 w-96 h-96 rounded-full"
   154‚Üí            style={{

   330‚Üí                  )}
   331‚Üí                  {secondaryAction && (
   332‚Üí                    <GlassButton
   333‚Üí                      variant="secondary"

   335‚Üí                      onClick={secondaryAction.onClick}

    24‚Üí */
    25‚Üíexport const AppleLiquidGlass = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, AppleLiquidGlassComponentProps>(
    26‚Üí  function AppleLiquidGlass({
    27‚Üí    children,
    28‚Üí    className = '',
    29‚Üí    contentClassName = '',
    30‚Üí    multiLayer = true,
    31‚Üí    intensity = 'medium',
    32‚Üí    interactive = true,
    33‚Üí    magnetic = false,
    34‚Üí    animated = false,
    35‚Üí    as: Component = 'div',
    36‚Üí    ...props
    37‚Üí  }, ref) {
    38‚Üí    const { ref: glassRef } = useAppleLiquidGlass({
    39‚Üí      intensity,
    40‚Üí      magneticStrength: magnetic ? 0.3 : 0,
    41‚Üí      liquidFlow: true,
    42‚Üí      enableHaptics: false,
    43‚Üí      multiLayer,
    44‚Üí      animated,
    45‚Üí      distortionEffect: true,
    46‚Üí    });
    47‚Üí
    48‚Üí    const glassClassName = getAppleLiquidGlassClass(intensity, {
    49‚Üí      interactive,
    50‚Üí      magnetic,
    51‚Üí      animated,
    52‚Üí      multiLayer,
    53‚Üí    });
    54‚Üí

    56‚Üí    const combinedRef = (element: HTMLDivElement | null) => {
    57‚Üí      if (typeof ref === 'function') {
    58‚Üí        ref(element);
    59‚Üí      } else if (ref) {
    60‚Üí        ref.current = element;
    61‚Üí      }
    62‚Üí

    64‚Üí        (glassRef as any).current = element;
    65‚Üí      }
    66‚Üí    };
    67‚Üí
    68‚Üí    const combinedClassName = `${glassClassName} ${className}`.trim();
    69‚Üí
    70‚Üí    if (multiLayer) {
    71‚Üí      return React.createElement(
    72‚Üí        Component,
    73‚Üí        {
    74‚Üí          ref: combinedRef,
    75‚Üí          className: combinedClassName,
    76‚Üí          ...props
    77‚Üí        },
    78‚Üí        createGlassLayers(children, contentClassName)
    79‚Üí      );
    80‚Üí    }
    81‚Üí
    82‚Üí    // Legacy single-layer implementation
    83‚Üí    return React.createElement(
    84‚Üí      Component,
    85‚Üí      {
    86‚Üí        ref: combinedRef,
    87‚Üí        className: combinedClassName,
    88‚Üí        ...props
    89‚Üí      },
    90‚Üí      children
    91‚Üí    );
    92‚Üí  }
    93‚Üí);

1‚Üí/**
     2‚Üí * Apple Liquid Glass Effects
     3‚Üí * Authentic Apple-style liquid glass implementation with physics-based interactions
     4‚Üí * Enhanced with React 19 patterns and multi-layer structure
     5‚Üí */
     6‚Üí
     7‚Üíimport React, { useRef, useEffect, useCallback, startTransition } from 'react';
     8‚Üí
     9‚Üíexport interface AppleLiquidGlassOptions {
    10‚Üí  intensity?: 'subtle' | 'medium' | 'strong';
    11‚Üí  magneticStrength?: number;
    12‚Üí  liquidFlow?: boolean;
    13‚Üí  enableHaptics?: boolean;
    14‚Üí  multiLayer?: boolean;
    15‚Üí  animated?: boolean;
    16‚Üí  distortionEffect?: boolean;
    17‚Üí}
    18‚Üí
    19‚Üíexport interface AppleLiquidGlassProps {
    20‚Üí  className?: string;
    21‚Üí  children?: React.ReactNode;
    22‚Üí  multiLayer?: boolean;
    23‚Üí  intensity?: 'subtle' | 'medium' | 'strong';
    24‚Üí  interactive?: boolean;
    25‚Üí  magnetic?: boolean;
    26‚Üí  animated?: boolean;
    27‚Üí}
    28‚Üí
    29‚Üíexport const APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = {
    30‚Üí  subtle: {
    31‚Üí    background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08)',
    32‚Üí    backdropFilter: 'blur(12px) saturate(150%)',
    33‚Üí    border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6)',
    34‚Üí    borderRadius: '24px',
    35‚Üí  },
    36‚Üí  medium: {
    37‚Üí    background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15)',
    38‚Üí    backdropFilter: 'blur(20px) saturate(180%)',
    39‚Üí    border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)',
    40‚Üí    borderRadius: '32px',
    41‚Üí  },
    42‚Üí  strong: {
    43‚Üí    background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.25)',
    44‚Üí    backdropFilter: 'blur(32px) saturate(200%)',
    45‚Üí    border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)',
    46‚Üí    borderRadius: '40px',
    47‚Üí  },
    48‚Üí} as const;
    49‚Üí
    50‚Üíexport const APPLE_LIQUID_SHADOWS = {
    51‚Üí  subtle: '0 4px 16px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.1), inset 0 2px 10px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)',
    52‚Üí  medium: '0 8px 32px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.2), inset 0 4px 20px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)',
    53‚Üí  strong: '0 16px 48px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.3), inset 0 8px 32px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.4)',
    54‚Üí} as const;
    55‚Üí
    56‚Üíexport const APPLE_LIQUID_AFTER_EFFECTS = {
    57‚Üí  subtle: {
    58‚Üí    boxShadow: 'inset -6px -4px 0px -7px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8), inset 0px -5px 0px -4px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)',
    59‚Üí    filter: 'blur(0.5px) drop-shadow(6px 2px 4px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)) brightness(110%)',
    60‚Üí  },
    61‚Üí  medium: {
    62‚Üí    boxShadow: 'inset -10px -8px 0px -11px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1), inset 0px -9px 0px -8px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1)',
    63‚Üí    filter: 'blur(1px) drop-shadow(10px 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)) brightness(115%)',
    64‚Üí  },
    65‚Üí  strong: {
    66‚Üí    boxShadow: 'inset -14px -12px 0px -15px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1), inset 0px -13px 0px -12px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1)',
    67‚Üí    filter: 'blur(1.5px) drop-shadow(14px 6px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4)) brightness(120%)',
    68‚Üí  },
    69‚Üí} as const;
    70‚Üí
    71‚Üí/**
    72‚Üí * Enhanced Hook for Apple liquid glass magnetic hover effect
    73‚Üí * Updated with React 19 patterns and performance optimizations
    74‚Üí */
    75‚Üíexport function useAppleLiquidGlass(options: AppleLiquidGlassOptions = {}) {
    76‚Üí  const elementRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
    77‚Üí  const {
    78‚Üí    intensity = 'medium',
    79‚Üí    magneticStrength = 0.3,
    80‚Üí    liquidFlow = true,
    81‚Üí    enableHaptics = false,
    82‚Üí    multiLayer = false,
    83‚Üí    animated = false,
    84‚Üí    distortionEffect = false,
    85‚Üí  } = options;
    86‚Üí
    87‚Üí  const handleMouseMove = useCallback((e: MouseEvent) => {
    88‚Üí    if (!elementRef.current) return;
    89‚Üí
    90‚Üí    // Use startTransition for smooth animations
    91‚Üí    startTransition(() => {
    92‚Üí      const rect = elementRef.current!.getBoundingClientRect();
    93‚Üí      const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
    94‚Üí      const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
    95‚Üí      
    96‚Üí      const deltaX = (e.clientX - centerX) * magneticStrength;
    97‚Üí      const deltaY = (e.clientY - centerY) * magneticStrength;
    98‚Üí
    99‚Üí      elementRef.current!.style.transform = `translate(${deltaX}px, ${deltaY}px) translateZ(0)`;
   100‚Üí      
   101‚Üí      if (liquidFlow && multiLayer) {
   102‚Üí        // Enhanced liquid flow for multi-layer structure
   103‚Üí        const glassFilter = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   104‚Üí        const glassOverlay = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   105‚Üí        
   106‚Üí        if (glassFilter) {
   107‚Üí          glassFilter.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.2}px, ${-deltaY * 0.2}px)`;
   108‚Üí        }
   109‚Üí        
   110‚Üí        if (glassOverlay) {
   111‚Üí          glassOverlay.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.1}px, ${-deltaY * 0.1}px)`;
   112‚Üí        }
   113‚Üí      }
   114‚Üí    });
   115‚Üí  }, [magneticStrength, liquidFlow, multiLayer]);
   116‚Üí
   117‚Üí  const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
   118‚Üí    if (!elementRef.current) return;
   119‚Üí    
   120‚Üí    startTransition(() => {
   121‚Üí      elementRef.current!.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) translateZ(0)';
   122‚Üí      elementRef.current!.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   123‚Üí      
   124‚Üí      if (multiLayer) {
   125‚Üí        const glassFilter = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   126‚Üí        const glassOverlay = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   127‚Üí        
   128‚Üí        if (glassFilter) {
   129‚Üí          glassFilter.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px)';
   130‚Üí          glassFilter.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   131‚Üí        }
   132‚Üí        
   133‚Üí        if (glassOverlay) {
   134‚Üí          glassOverlay.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px)';
   135‚Üí          glassOverlay.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   136‚Üí        }
   137‚Üí      }
   138‚Üí      
   139‚Üí      setTimeout(() => {
   140‚Üí        if (elementRef.current) {
   141‚Üí          elementRef.current.style.transition = '';
   142‚Üí          
   143‚Üí          if (multiLayer) {
   144‚Üí            const glassFilter = elementRef.current.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   145‚Üí            const glassOverlay = elementRef.current.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   146‚Üí            
   147‚Üí            if (glassFilter) glassFilter.style.transition = '';
   148‚Üí            if (glassOverlay) glassOverlay.style.transition = '';
   149‚Üí          }
   150‚Üí        }
   151‚Üí      }, 500);
   152‚Üí    });
   153‚Üí
   154‚Üí    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   155‚Üí      navigator.vibrate(10);
   156‚Üí    }
   157‚Üí  }, [enableHaptics, multiLayer]);
   158‚Üí
   159‚Üí  const handleMouseEnter = useCallback(() => {
   160‚Üí    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   161‚Üí      navigator.vibrate(5);
   162‚Üí    }
   163‚Üí  }, [enableHaptics]);
   164‚Üí
   165‚Üí  useEffect(() => {
   166‚Üí    const element = elementRef.current;
   167‚Üí    if (!element) return;
   168‚Üí
   169‚Üí    element.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   170‚Üí    element.addEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   171‚Üí    element.addEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   172‚Üí
   173‚Üí    return () => {
   174‚Üí      element.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   175‚Üí      element.removeEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   176‚Üí      element.removeEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   177‚Üí    };
   178‚Üí  }, [handleMouseMove, handleMouseLeave, handleMouseEnter]);
   179‚Üí
   180‚Üí  return {
   181‚Üí    ref: elementRef,
   182‚Üí    variant: APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS[intensity],
   183‚Üí    shadow: APPLE_LIQUID_SHADOWS[intensity],
   184‚Üí    afterEffect: APPLE_LIQUID_AFTER_EFFECTS[intensity],
   185‚Üí    multiLayer,
   186‚Üí    animated,
   187‚Üí    distortionEffect,
   188‚Üí  };
   189‚Üí}
   190‚Üí
   191‚Üí/**
   192‚Üí * Generate Apple liquid glass CSS classes - Tailwind v4 Compatible
   193‚Üí * Enhanced with multi-layer and new effect options
   194‚Üí */
   195‚Üíexport function getAppleLiquidGlassClass(
   196‚Üí  intensity: keyof typeof APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = 'medium',
   197‚Üí  options: {
   198‚Üí    interactive?: boolean;
   199‚Üí    magnetic?: boolean;
   200‚Üí    animated?: boolean;
   201‚Üí    multiLayer?: boolean;
   202‚Üí  } = {}
   203‚Üí): string {
   204‚Üí  const { interactive = true, magnetic = false, animated = false, multiLayer = false } = options;
   205‚Üí  
   206‚Üí  const baseClass = 'apple-liquid-glass';
   207‚Üí  const intensityClass = intensity !== 'medium' ? `apple-liquid-glass--${intensity}` : '';
   208‚Üí  const interactiveClass = interactive ? 'apple-liquid-glass--interactive' : '';
   209‚Üí  const magneticClass = magnetic ? 'apple-liquid-glass--magnetic' : '';
   210‚Üí  const animatedClass = animated ? 'apple-liquid-glass--animated' : '';
   211‚Üí  
   212‚Üí  return [baseClass, intensityClass, interactiveClass, magneticClass, animatedClass].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
   213‚Üí}
   214‚Üí
   215‚Üí/**
   216‚Üí * Generate multi-layer glass structure JSX
   217‚Üí * For use with the new multi-layer glass components
   218‚Üí */
   219‚Üíexport function createGlassLayers(content: React.ReactNode, className?: string): React.ReactNode {
   220‚Üí  return React.createElement(
   221‚Üí    React.Fragment,
   222‚Üí    null,
   223‚Üí    React.createElement('div', { className: 'glass-filter' }),
   224‚Üí    React.createElement('div', { className: 'glass-overlay' }),
   225‚Üí    React.createElement('div', { className: 'glass-specular' }),
   226‚Üí    React.createElement('div', { className: `glass-content ${className || ''}` }, content)
   227‚Üí  );
   228‚Üí}
   229‚Üí
   230‚Üí/**
   231‚Üí * Apple liquid glass animation presets
   232‚Üí */
   233‚Üíexport const APPLE_LIQUID_ANIMATIONS = {
   234‚Üí  hover: {
   235‚Üí    transform: 'translateY(-2px)',
   236‚Üí    transition: 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   237‚Üí  },
   238‚Üí  active: {
   239‚Üí    transform: 'translateY(0px) scale(0.98)',
   240‚Üí    transition: 'all 0.15s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   241‚Üí  },
   242‚Üí  focus: {
   243‚Üí    boxShadow: '0 0 0 3px rgba(0, 122, 255, 0.3)',
   244‚Üí    transition: 'box-shadow 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   245‚Üí  },
   246‚Üí} as const;
```
